* Fairchild Semiconductor Trench IGBT FS4 SQD 650V
* Last Update: May 16, 2016
* Models developed and verified with PSPICE 16.6/LTSPICE IV/Simetrix 7.20
* Usage:
* This library contains 3 and 6 pin(or terminal) models. 
* The 3p models are isothermal with self-heating effects turned off.
* The 6p models are electro-thermal and contain additional pins: 
* tji/tjd (or junction temperature of igbt and diode)
* tcase (or device case thermal terminal).
* tj pins should always be left floating or can be connected to a very
* large resistor (>1meg). This terminal is meant to provide the user with
* output information on the junction temperature under operation. For model
* verification purposes against the data sheet and isothermal device simulations
* for example, tcase should be connected to a "E" voltage source with value {TEMP},
* the simulator ambient temperature. For system/module level simulations that
* include thermal effects, tcase should be connected to the device-module
* thermal interface node such as the heat sink interface point.
*
* In the case a designer wished to bypass the internal ZTH network, tj should be
* shorted to tcase and then tcase connected to the user defined ZTH network.
*
*
* Models work in conjunction with pspice FAIRCHILD_IGBT_FS4SQD650.OLB symbol library
* Models work in conjunction with ltspice FGY120T65SP(D)_F085_rev1_ltspice_symbols.zip symbol library
* Models work in conjunction with simetrix IGBT-Symbols.sxslb symbol library
* Stand alone usage:
* subcircuit instance statement: 
* Xname c g e <devname_3p>
* Xname c g e tji tjd tcase <devname_6p>
*
*
* Supported Devices (devname):
* FGH75T65SQD_F155_3P
* FGH75T65SQD_F155_6P

*
